වාර්ෂක වාරතාව                                                                                                              2017

දැක්ම, මෙහෙවර, අරමුණු

 දැක්ම

ශි ලංකාව තුළ යීවර යාත්‍රා සහ විනෝද යාත්‍රා නිෂ්පාදනයේ මෙන්ම අනෙකුත්‌ ෆයිබර්‌ ග්ලාස්‌ ආශිත
නිෂ්පාදන වල ප්‍රමුඛයා බවට පත්‌ වීම හා ජාත්‍යන්තර වශයෙන්‌ පිළිගත්‌ යාත්‍රා නිෂ්පාදකයකු බවට පත්‌
වීම.

~ මෙහෙවර

තරඟකාරී මිල ගණන්‌ යටතේ ඉහළ ප්‍රමිතියකින්‌ යුතු ධිවර යාත්‍රා සහ ධීවර ආම්පන්න සපයන
කාටයක්ෂම හා ඵළදායී ආයතනයක්‌ ලෙස කටයුතු කිරීම.

_ අරමුණු

* ෆයිබට ග්ලාස්‌ බෝටිටූ අපනයනයේ පිළිගත්‌ අපනයනකරැවෙකු බවට පත්‌ වීම.

* ජාත්‍යන්තරයේ කීරිතිමත්‌ ෆයිබට ග්ලාස්‌ බෝටිටූ නිෂ්පාදකයෙකු බවට පත්‌ වීම.

* විදේශ රටවල්‌ තුළ ෆයිබර්‌ ග්ලාස්‌ බෝටිටූ නිෂ්පාදනයේ අආයෝජිතයෙකු බවට පත්‌ වීම.
* විශෂ්ඨ පාරිභෝගික සේවා සපයන්නෙක වීම.

04. මූලික මෙහෙයුම්‌ කාරයයන්‌
2017 වරීෂයෙහි සමාගමේ මූලික මෙහෙයුම්‌ කාරියයන්‌ පහත පරිදි දැක්වේ.

0 සියලූ පහසුකම්‌ වලින්‌ සමන්විත ෆයිබර්‌ ග්ලාස්‌ බහුදින ධිවර යාත්‍රා නිෂ්පාදනය.

ං එක්දින ෆයිබට ග්ලාස්‌ ධිවර යාත්‍රා නිෂ්පාදනය.

ෆං ධීවර කටමාන්තය සඳහා අවශ්‍ය මාල පෙට්ටි අලෙවි කුටි සහ ආරක්ෂක කුටි

ට මිරිදිය ධිවර කටමාන්තයට අවශ්‍ය ඔරැ සහ කොල්ලෑ නිෂ්පාදනය කිරීම.

ං ධීවර ක්ෂේත්‍රයට අවශ්‍ය මාළු දැල්‌ සහ ඒ ආශිත උපකරණ මිලදී ගැනීම සහ විකිණීම

0 සංචාරක ක්ෂේත්‍රයට අවශ්‍ය විනෝද යාත්‍රා සහ තල්මසුන්‌ නැරඹීමේ යාත්‍රා නිෂ්පාදනය

ක්‌ වන ගබඩා සංකීරීණය නිවැරදි ප්‍රසම්පාදන කබ්‍රයාවලීන්‌ අනුගමනය කර රජයේ තක්සේ්‍රැ
මුදලට වඩා වැඩි මිලකට කුලී පදනම මත ලබා දීමට සැලසුම්‌ කර ඇත.

සීමාසහිත සීනොෝට පදනම සතුව පැවැති

බෝට්ටු යාත්‍රාංගනයෙහි ඉදිකිරීම්‌ කටයුතු
මේ වන විට අවසාන අදියරට පැමිණ ඇත.
ශක්‍යතා අධ්‍යයන වාරතාව ලබා ගැනීමෙන්‌      ක    ක

සැලසුම්‌ කර ඇත.

සඳහා අවශ්‍ය සියළුම තොරතුරු සහ පැහැදිලි කිරීම්‌ මා විසින්‌ ලබාගන්නා ලද බවත්‌, මාගේ

පරීක්ෂණවලින්‌ පෙනීයන අන්දමට සමාගම විසින්‌ වියිමත්‌ ගිණුමිකරණ වාර්තා පවත්වා ඇති

බවත්‌,

සමාගමේ මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන 2007 අංක 07 දරන සමාගම්‌ පනතේ 151 වගන්තියෙහි අවශ්‍යතාවයන්ට

අනුකුල වන බවත්‌ මා දරන්නා චූ මතය වේ.

වාර්ෂික වාර්තා සභාගත කිරීම

ශී ලංකා ප්‍රජාතාන්ත්‍රික සමාජවාදී ජනරජයේ ආණ්ඩුක්‍රම ව්‍යවස්ථාවේ 154 (6) වා්‍යවස්ථාවෙගි ඇතුළත්‌

විධිවිධාන ප්‍රකාරව මාගේ වාර්තාව යථා කාලයේදී පාර්ලිමේන්තුවේ සහාගත කරනු ලැබේ.

මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහ ප්‍රකාශය

2017 දෙසැම්බර්‌ 31 වන දිනෙන්‌ අවසන්‌ වර්ෂය

(සියලු අංක රැපියල්‌ වලිනි)

කාරක ප්‍රාග්ධන වියදම්‌ වලට පෙර

තොගවල අඩු කිරීම / වැඩි කිරීම්‌

වෙළඳ හා අනෙකුත්‌ ලැබීම්‌ වල අඩු කිරීම්‌ ” වැඩි
කිරීමි

වෙළඳ හා අනෙකුත්‌ ගෙවීම්‌ වල අඩු කිරීම්‌ ” වැඩි

කිරීම

විලමිභිත ආදායම්‌ අඩු කිරීම ” වැඩි කිරීම්‌
මෙහෙයුම්‌ ක්‍රියාවලින්‌ උත්පාදනය කල මුදල්‌
අධඩුකලා :

ආයෝජන ආදායම්‌

ආදායම්‌ බද ගෙවීම්‌

පාර්තෝෂිත ගෙවීම්‌

මෙහෙයුම්‌ ක්‍රියා වලින්‌ උත්පාදනය කරන ලද දල

2.1.2

සංයුක්ත තොරතුරැ
පිහිටීම හා නිතීමය තත්ත්වය

සීමා සහිත සීනොට පදනම ශී ලංකාව තුල සංස්ථාගත කළ සමාගමකි. ලියාපදිංචි
කාරයාලය අංක 335 ඞී. අආටී. විජේවර්ධන මාවත කොළඹ 10 යන ස්ථානයේ

පිහිටා ඇති අතර ප්‍රධාන බෝට්ටු යාත්‍රාංගනය මටිටක්කුලිය ප්‍රදේශයේ පිහිටා ඇත.
සිල්ලර අලෙවිසැල්‌ තංගල්ල සහ පෑලියගොඩ ප්‍රදේශවල පිහිටා ඇත.

ප්‍රධාන කියාකාරකම්‌ සහ මෙහෙයවීම

රාජ්‍ය සහ පෞද්ගලික ආයතනවල ඇණවුම්‌ වලට අනුව යාත්‍රාංගනයේ නිෂ්පාදනය
කරන ලද යාත්‍රා සහ භාණ්ඩ අලෙවිය සහ අනෙකුත්‌ ධීවර ආම්පන්න මිලදී ගැනීම
සහ අලෙවි කිරීම්‌ ලෙස සඳහන්‌ කල හැක.

ව්‍යෟවසායිකත්වයේ අයිතිය

පූටණ රජය සතු සමාගමකි.

සේවක සංඛ්‍යාව

වර්ෂය අවසාන වන විට සමාගමේ සේවක සංඛ්‍යාව 86 ක්‌ විය.

වැදගත්‌ ගිණුම්‌ ප්‍රතිපත්තිවල සාරාංශය
2.1 සාමාන්‍ය ප්‍රතිපත්ති
සැකසීමේ පදනම

2017 දෙසැම්බර්‌ 31 වන දිනට අවසන්‌ වූ වරෂය සඳහා වන සමාගමේ මුල්‍ය්‌
තත්ත්වය පිළිබඳ ප්‍රකාශනය සමස්ථ ආදායම්‌ ප්‍රකාශනය ව්‍යාපාර වස්තු කොටස්‌
අයිතිය සහ මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහ සහ ගිණුම්‌ ප්‍රතිපත්ති සහ සටහන්‌ (මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන ශී
ලංකා ගිණුම්‌ ප්‍රමිතීන්‌ සමග අනුගතවේ.

ශී ලංකා රැපියල්‌ වලින්‌ දක්වා ඇති මෙම මුල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන වෛතිහාසික පිරිවැය
පදනම මත සකස්‌ කර ඇත. මෙම මුල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන දඋද්ධමනකාරී සාධක වල
බලපෑම්‌ වලින්‌ තොරව සකස්‌ කර ඇත.

ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රතිපත්ති වල වෙනස්‌ වීමි සහ සංශෝධනය කරන ලද ශී ලංකා

ගිණුමිකරණ ප්‍රතිපත්ති සමග අනුගත වීම

වර්ෂය තුල නව සහ සංශෝධිත ග්‍රී ලංකා ගණකාධිකරණ පුමිතීන්‌ අනුගමනය
කිරීම.

පෙර වර්ෂවල අනුගමනය කළ ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රතිපත්ති මේ වර්ෂයේ ද නොවෙනස්ව
පැවතින.

338


වාර්ෂක වාරතාව                                                                                                       2017

2.1.3 සංසන්දනාත්මක තොරතුරැ

සමාගම විසින්‌ ප්‍රමාණවත්‌ පරිදි යොදා ගත්‌ ගිණුම්‌ ප්‍රතිපත්ති පෙර වර්ෂයේ දී
යොදා ගත්‌ ගිණුම්‌ ප්‍රතිපත්ති වලට අනුකල වේ. පෙර වර්ෂයේ වාරටතා වුණු සංඛ්‍යා
හා වාක්‍යයන්‌ මෙම වාරටතා වලට උවිත වන පරිදි නැවත සකස්‌ කර ඇත.

2.1.4 විදේශ මුදල්‌ ගනුදෙනු

සියලම විදේශ විනිමය ගනුදෙනු සිදුවන අවස්ථාවේදී පැවති විදේශ විනිමය
අනුපාතිකයට අනුව ශී ලංකා රැපියල්‌ වලට මාරැ කරනු ලැබේ. විදේශ මුදල්‌ ඒකක
වලින්‌ දක්වා ඇති මුල්‍ය වත්කම්‌ සහ බැරකම්‌ වරෂය අවසානයේ පැවැති විදේශ
විනිමය අනුපාතිකයන්ට අනුකුල වන සේ ශී ලංකා රැපියල්‌ වලට වරීෂ අවසානයේ
පැවති ස්ථානීය විනිමය අනුපාතිකයට අනුකුල වන සේ නැවත අආගනනය කරනු
ලැබේ. මෙහි ප්‍රතිඵලයක්‌ වශයෙන්‌ අත්කරගත්‌ ලාභය හෝ අලාභය ආදායම්‌
ප්‍රකාශනයට ඇතුලත්‌ කර ඇත.

2.1.5 බදිකරණය

වත්මන්‌ බදු

ආදායම්‌ බදු සඳහා වන පතිපාදන මුල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන වල දක්වා ඇති ආකාරයට
2006 අංක 10 දරණ දේශීය ආදායම්‌ පනතේ විධිවිධානයන්ට අනුකලවන සේ
ගණනය කර සමාගමට අදාල කරගත යුතු අනුපාතිකයට අනුව සිදිකර ඇත.

2.1.6 ශේෂ පතුය දිනයට පසුව සිදු කළ කියාකාරකම්‌

ගශේෂපතු දිනයට පසුව සිදු කරන ලද සියලුම ප්‍රධාන කියාකාරකම්‌ සලකා බලන
ලද අතර මුල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන වල ඒ සඳහා අවශ්‍ය ගැලපීම සිදු කොට ඇත.

2.1.7 ණය ගැනුම්‌ පිරිවැය

කාල පරිච්ඡේදය තුල දී ණය ගැනීම සඳහා වියදම ණය ගැනුම්‌ පිරිවැය ලෙස
සලකන ලදී.

2.2 වත්කම්‌ තක්සේ්‍රැ කිරීම හා ඒවා ගණනය කිරීමේ පදනම
2.2.1 භාණ්ඩ ලේඛන

භාණ්ඩ ගණනය කරනු ලබන්නේ ශුද්ධ උපලබිධි අගය හෝ අඩු වූ පිරිවැයෙන්‌
අභාවිත හෝ හෙමින්‌ නිකුත්‌ වන භාණඩ වල වටිනාකම්‌ ගැලපීමෙනි. සාමාන්‍ය
ව්‍යාපාරික කටයුතු වලදී විකිණීම සිදු කරන්නේ භාණ්ඩ නිම කිරීමේ පිරිවැය
ගැලැපජීමෙන්‌ ලැබෙන ශුද්ධ උපලබදි වටිනාකමය. වරතමාන ස්ථානයට මෙම
භාණඩ තොගය ගෙන ඒමේදී වැය වූ පිරිවැය සහ එහි තත්වය පහත සඳහන්‌
සුත්‍රය මඟින්‌ ගණනය කරනු ලැබේ.

අමුදිව්‍ය්‌               -      පළමු ලැබීම්‌ පලමු නිකුත්‌ කිරීම්‌ මත සත්‍ය පිරිවැය

නිශ්පාදිත නිම්‌ භාණ්ඩ -     සෘජු අමුදුව්‍ය වල සත්‍ය පිරිවැය නිම කල භාණ්ඩ
වල ප්‍රතිශතය අනුව සෘජු ශුමය හා ස්ථාවර පොද
කාර්යයෙන්‌ අදාල පිරිවැය

2.2.2 මූල්‍ය වත්කම්‌

වෙළඳ සහ වෙනත්‌ ලැබිය යුතු දෑ මුලදී මිලට පිළිගනු ලැබේ. සියලූ විකුණුම්‌
සාමාන්‍ය ණයවර නියමයන්‌ මත කරනු ලබන අතර ලැබිය යුතු දේ සඳහා කිසිඳ
පොළයක්‌ අය නොකෙරේ. සෑම වාරතා කිරීම්‌ කාල වකවානුවේ අවසානයේදී මුදල්‌
අයකර ගත නොහැකි බවට බාහිර සාක්ෂි තිබේද යන්න තීරණය කිරීමට වාණිජ
ධාරණ මුදල්‌ සහ වෙනත්‌ අයවිය යුතු දේ පරික්ෂා කරනු ලැබේ. එසේ ඇත්නම්‌
ලාහ හෝ අලාභ හානි කරන අලාභයක්‌ සඳහා ගනී.

මුදල්‌ සහ මුදල්‌ සමාන වත්කම්‌ අතැති මුදල්‌ ඉල්ලුම්‌ තැන්පතු සහ කෙටි කාලීන
දිව්‍යශිලිතාවයෙන්‌ අග්‍ර ආයෝජන සෂණිකව මුදල්‌ බවට පත්‌ කල හැකි දේ වන
අතර වටිනාකම කිසිම විධියේ අවදානමකට භාජනය නොවන්නෙකි. මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවහ
පිකාශනවලට අඇැතැම්‌ මුදල්‌ සහ බැංකු තැන්පතු අයිරාවල ශුද්ධ හිඟ මුදල්‌,
කෙටිකාලීනව මෝරන ආයෝජන වන අතර ඒවා මාස 3 ක්‌ හෝ අත්පත්‌ කර ගත්‌

දිනට අඩු නම්‌ මුදල්‌ සමාන වත්කම්‌ ලෙස සලකනු ලබයි.

2.2.3 දේපළ පිරියත සහ උපකරණ
(ආ තක්සේ්‍රැ පිරිවැය

සියළුම දේපළ පිරියත හා උපකරණ මුලික අවස්ථාවේ ගණනය කරනු ලබන්නේ
පිරවැයෙනි. දේපළ පිරියත හා උපකරණ වල පිරිවැය යනු වත්කම එහි වරතමාන
තත්ත්වයට සහ ස්ථානයට ගෙන ඒම සඳහා දරන ලද මිලදී ගැනීමේ හා ඉදිකිරීමට
අදාල සියලූ වියදම්‌ වේ.

දේපළ පිරියත හා උපකරණ සමුච්චිත ක්ෂය හා සමුච්චිත හානිකරණ අගයට වඩා
අඩු පිරිවැයෙන්‌ මනිනු ලැබේ.

දේපළ පිරියත හා උපකරණ පසුකාලීනව දරණ ප්‍රාග්ධන වියදම්‌ ලෙස හඳනාගනු
ලබන්නේ එම වියදම්‌ මගින්‌ මෙම වත්කම්‌ වල ක්‍රියාකාරිත්වය වැඩිදියුණු වීමක්‌ සහ
ඒ හා බැඳුණු අනාගත ප්‍රතිඵල ආයතනයට ගලා ඒමක්‌ සිදු වනවානම්‌ පමණි.

(ආ සෂය කිරීම්‌

(අ) මූල්‍ය නොවන වත්කම්‌ හානිකරණය

සෑම වාරතා කිරීමේ දිනට එවැනි වත්කම්‌ හානිකරණයට ලක්‌ වී ඇති බවට කිසිැද
සාක්ෂයක්‌ ඇත්දැයි තීරණය කිරීමට දේපළ පරික්ෂා කරනු ලැබේ. සිදුවිය හැකි
හානිය පිළිබඳ ඇඟවීමක්‌ තිබේනම්‌ අදාළ වත්කමේ (හෝ අදාළ වත්කම්‌
කාණ්ඩයේ) අය කර ගත හැකි අගය තක්සේ්‍රැ කරනු ලබන අතර එහි ධාරණ
අගයට සසඳනු ලැබේ. නිමිත අයකර ගත හැකි අගය නම්‌ ධාරණ අගය එහි නිමිත
අයකර ගත හැකි අගයට අඩු කරනු ලබන අතර හානිකරණ අලාභයත්‌
හඳනාගතහැකි විස්තීටරණ ආදායමේ ප්‍රකාශනයට ඇතුලත්‌ කරනු ලැබේ.

සමාගමේ වත්කම්‌ සෑම කුයාත්මක දිනයකදීම ඒවායේ බෙලහීන තත්වය ගැන දැන
ගැනීමට හැකිවේ. එසේ බෙලහීන තත්වයක්‌ ඇත්නම්‌ වාරීෂක බෙලහීන තත්වය
සොයා බැලීමේ පරීඤක්‍ෂණයකදී එම වත්කම්‌ වලින්‌ ආපසු ලබා ගත හැකි වටිනාකම
ගැන තක්සේර්‍රැවක්‌ කරනු ලැබේ. එම වත්කම්‌ වලින්‌ ලබා ගත හැකි වටිනාකම
එම වත්කම සාධාරණ තක්සේ්‍රැ වටිනාකමින්‌ විකුණුම්‌ පිරිවැය අඩුකල විට එම
වටිනාකමේ අගය තීරණය කරනු ලැබේ. එම වත්කම්‌ වටිනාකම ලබාගත හැකි
වටිනාකමේ බෙලහීනතාව ගැන සලකා බලා අයකරගත නොහැකි වටිනාකම ලියා
හරිනු ලැබේ.

එම වත්කමේ භාවිත වටිනාකමින්‌ ලැබෙන අනාගත මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය වත්මන්‌
වටිනාකමට පෙර බද වටිටමි්‌ අනුපාතයෙන්‌ වටිටම්‌ කල හොත්‌ වත්කම්‌
වෙළදපොලේ වටිනාකමත්‌, වත්මන්‌ මුදලේ වටිනාකමත්‌ එම වත්කමේ දැරීමේ
අවදානම ගැනත්‌ දැනගත හැකිය.

ආදායම්‌ ප්‍රකාශනයක හානිකර අලාභය බෙලහීන උපකරණ වල හානිකර අලාභයට
පෙර ප්‍රත්‍යාගණන සංචිතයට පුතිවිරැද්ධ ලෙස ගැලපිය යුතුය. සෑම වාරටතා කරන
දිනට තක්ස්‍රැවක්‌ කරනූ ලබන්නේ පෙරදී තක්සේ්‍රැ කළ හානිකර අලාභය
නොපැවතීම හෝ අඩුකර දැක්වීමය. පෙරදින හඳනාගත්‌ හානිකර අලාභය
කිටතිනාමය හැරැණුවිට වත්කමින්‌ නැවත අයකර ගත හැකි මුදල වැඩි වී ඇත්නම්‌
වත්කමට ගලපනු ලැබේ. පෙර හඳනාගත්‌ හානිකර අලාභයට බලපෑමක්‌ නොවේ
නම වත්කමේ වැඩි වීමක්‌ ලෙස හඳනාගනු ලැබේ.

2.3 වගකීම හා වෙන්‌ කිරීම්‌
2.3.1 විශ්‍රාම ප්‍රතිලාභ බැදීම්‌
(ආ නිශ්චිත පාරතෝෂත ප්‍රතිලාභ සැලසුම

පාරතෝෂත දීමනා සැලසුම්‌ කල පුතිලාභහයකි. සමාගමට පාරතෝෂත දීමනා
පනතට අනුව ගෙවීමට හැකියාවක්‌ ඇත. මෙම වගකීම දැරීම සඳහා ශේෂ පත්‍රයේ
ඉදිරයට ගෙන අආ වෙන්‌ කිරීමක්‌ මුදල්‌ වර්ෂයේ අවසානයේ ලබාගත්‌ වැටුපෙන්‌
වර්ෂයකට මාස භාගයක වැටුපට සමාන වත ලෙස සේවා කාලය ආරම්භයේ සිට
අදාල මුදල්‌ වර්ෂය තෙක්‌ ගනනය කර වෙන්‌ කිරීමි සිදු කරයි. ඉදිරිය ගෙන ආ


වෙන්‌ කිරීම වර්ෂය ආරම්භයේ ඇති වෙන්‌ කිරීමේ ශේෂයට ගලපා වෙනස ආදායම්‌
ප්‍රකාශනයට ඇතුලත්‌ කරනු ලැබේ.

1083 අංක 12 දරණ පනතේ වගන්තිවලට අනුකුලව වගකීම දැරීය යුත්තේ
අබණ්ඩ සේවා කාලය වරීෂ 5 සම්පුටිණ කිරීමෙන්‌ පසුවය. පාරතොෝමෂත වගකිම

අරමුදල්‌ ලැබීමක්‌ හෝ සත්‍ය ගනනය කිරීමක්‌ නොවේ. මෙම අයිතමය විලම්භිත
වගකිමක්‌ ලෙස ශේෂ පත්‍රයේ දක්වයි.

(ආ නිශ්චිත දායකත්ව සැලසුම්‌ - සේවක අර්ථසාධක සහ සේවක භාරකාර අරමුදල්‌

නිශ්චිත දායකත්ව සැලසුම සේවා අටිථ සාධක අරමුදල සහ සේවා භාරකාරථත්ව
අරමුදල අදාල අනපනත්‌ වල වගන්ති අනුව සියම සේවකයින්‌ අටඊථ සාධක
අරමුදලේ සහ සේවා භාර කාරීත්ව අරමුදලේ දායක්තවයෙන්‌ ආවරණය විය යුතුය.

සේවක අටථසාධක අරමුදල

අනුමත සේවක අථටථසාධක අරමුදලට එක්‌ එක්‌ සේවකයාගේ වැටුපෙන්‌ සහ
සමාගම විසින්‌ පිළිවෙලින්‌ 12% ක්‌ සහ 80% ක්‌ වශයෙන්‌ දායකත්වය දක්වනු
ලැබේ.

සේවක භාරකාර අරමුදල

සේවක භාරකාර අරමුදල සඳහා සමාගම විසින්‌ එක්‌ එක්‌ සේවකයාගේ වැටුපෙන්‌
30% ක්‌ වශයෙන්‌ දායකත්වය දක්වනු ලැබේ.

2.3.2 මූල්‍ය වගකීම්‌

මූල්‍ය වගකීම්‌ (ගනුදෙනු පිරිවැය අඇැතුළත්වා ගනුදෙනු වියදම්‌ මත මුලිකව
හඳනාගනු ලැබේ. ගෙවිය යුතු දෑ සාමාන්‍ය ණය කාලසීමාව සඳහා ඇති බැඳීම්‌ වන
අතර ඒ සඳහා කිසිඳු පොළියක්‌ නැත.

2.3.3 ප්‍රාග්ධන යෙදවුම්‌ හා අවිනිශ්චිත අවශ්‍යතා

ගශේෂපතු්‍රු දිනට ඇති ප්‍රාග්ධන යෙදවුම්‌ හා අවිනිෂ්චිත වගකීම්‌ සියල්ල මූල්‍ය
ප්‍රකාශනයේ සටහන්‌ මගින්‌ දක්වා අත. (සටහන 27)

2.3.4 ප්‍රතිපාදන

අතීත සිදවීම්වල ප්‍රතිඵල ලෙස සමාගමට ඇති වරිතමාන බැඳියාව (නීත්‍යානුකල
හෝ සාධනීය) දරන විට පුතිපාදනයන්‌ ලෙස පිළිගනු ලබයි. තවද සමාගම විසින්‌
වගකිම ඉටුකළ යුතු අතර වගකීමේ අගය සඳහා විශ්වාසදායක තක්සේ්‍රැවක්‌ කළ
හැකිය.

මෙම මුදල හඳනාගනු ලබන්නේ වගකීම වටා ඇති අවදානම්‌ හා අවිනිශ්චිතතාව
සැලකිල්ලට ගෙන මූල්‍ය තත්ත්ව ප්‍රකාශනයේ වරිතමාන වගකීම ඉටු කිරීමට ලබා
දිය හැකි හොඳම තක්ස්‍රැව ලෙසය.

2.4 ආදායම්‌ ප්‍රකාශය

2.4.1 ආදායම්‌ හඳනා ගැනීම

ආදායම වශයෙන්‌ හඳනා ගනු ලබන ප්‍රමාණයට සමාගමට ගලා එන අඩමාන
ආදායම හා අදායමට සම්බන්ධ වන දරන ලද පිරවැය හෝ දැරයයුතු පිරවැයේ
විශ්වාසනීයත්වය ගනනය කිරීමයි.

                    E


වාර්ෂක වාරතාව                                                                                                       2017

(4) භාණ්ඩ විකිණීම

භාණ්ඩ විකුණුම්‌ හඳනා ගනු ලබන්නේ සැලකිය යුතු අවදානම සහ භාණ්ඩ
භාරකාරිත්වයේ වාසිය සමාගමෙන්‌ ගැනුම්‌ කරැවා වෙත නිකුත්වීමේදී රඳවා
නොගත්‌ අයිතිය සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ වූ ආර්ථික සබැඳියාව හෝ විකුණු භාණ්ඩයේ
පාලනයයි.

(5) පොලිය
උපචිත පදනම මත පොලිය හඳනා ගනු ලැබේ.

(0) බඳු කුලී ආදායම
උපචිත පදනම මත බද කුලී හඳනා ගනු ලැබේ.

(0d) අනෙකුත්‌ ආදායම්‌
අනෙකුත්‌ ආදායම උපචිත පදනම මත හඳනා ගනු ලැබේ.

(€) ලාභසහ පාඩු

ශුද්ධ ලාහ හා පාඩු දේපල උපලබිදිය කදී යන්ත්‍ර උපකරණ ආදායම්‌ ප්‍රකාශනයට
ගනු ලබන්නේ අපහරන වියදම්‌ විකිණීමෙන්‌ ලැබෙන මුදලින්‌ අඩු කිරීමෙන්‌ පසු,
දේපලේ අගය ලෙස ගනන්‌ ගනු ලබන්නේ අදාල දේපලහේ උපලබිදි වියදම්‌
විකුණුම්‌ වියදම්‌ අඩු කිරමෙනි ප්‍රත්‍යාගනන සංචිත ගිණුමේ ඉතිරවන ශේෂය
කෙලින්ම සමුච්චිත ලාභයට මාරැ කරනු ලැබේ.

(7) රජයේප්‍රධාන

අදාල පුධානය ලැබෙන බවට සහ එම ප්‍රධානයට ඇතුලත්‌ කොන්දේසි වලට
අනුකුලව ආයතනය කටයුතු කරන බවට සාධාරණ සහතිකයක්‌ ඇත්නම්‌, එම
ලැබීම්‌ රාජ්‍ය ප්‍රධාන ලෙස හඳනා ගනු ලබයි. විලමිභීත ආදායමක්‌ ලෙස
හඳුනාගන්නා වත්කම්‌ වලට අදාල ප්‍රුධානයන්‌ එම වත්කම්‌ ක්ෂය කරනු ලබන
කාලපරිච්ඡේදය තුල කාලසීමාවේ ලාභයට හෝ අලාභයට සමානුපාතිකව ගලපනු
ලබයි.

2.4.2 වියදම්‌ හඳනා ගැනීම

ආදායම්‌ ප්‍රකාශනයේ වියදමේ පදනම ලෙස හඳුනාගනු ලබන්නේ දරණ ලද
පිරවැයත්‌ ඉපැයූ විශේෂිත අයිතම්වල ආදායම අතර වෙනසකි. ව්‍යාපාරය
කාරීයයෂමව පවත්වාගෙන යාමේදී දැරැ සියළු වියදම්‌ සහ දේපල යන්ත්‍ර සුත්‍ර
නඩත්තුවට දැරැ වියදම්‌ වරෂයේ ලාහය නිශ්චය කිරීම සඳහා ආදායම්‌
ප්‍රකාශනයට මාරැ කරයි.

2.4.3 ඇස්තමේන්තුගත අවිනිශ්චිතතාවයේ විවේචනාත්මක විනිශ්චයන්‌ සහ ප්‍රධාන
මූලාශ

සමාගමේ මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන සැකසීමේදී වාරතාකිරීමේ දිනට ආදායමේ වාරිතාගත
මුදල, වියදම්‌, වත්කම්‌ සහ අනිශ්චිත වගකීම හෙළිකිරීම වැනිදේට බලපාන
විනිශ්ව, තක්සේ්‍රැ සහ උපකල්පන කිරීමට කළමනාකාරීත්වයට සිදු වේ.

සටහන 25 - රජයේ ප්‍රධාන

A.   අදාළ වත්කම්‌ වල ප්‍රයෝජනවත්‌ ජීවිත කාලය වෙනුවෙන්‌ විස්තීරණ ආදායම්‌
ප්‍රකාශනයේ වත්කමට අදාළ රජයේ පුතිපාදනයක්‌ ලෙස හඳනාගන්නා ලදී මූල්‍ය
වසරේදී වෙනත්‌ මෙහෙයුම්‌ ආදායම්‌ යටතේ විස්තීටණ ආදායම්‌ ප්‍රකාශනයේ
රැ. 11,315,087.89 ක්‌ හඳනාගන්නා ලදී එම කාල වකවානුවේ ආදායමක්‌ ලෙස

පිළිනොගන්නා ලද රජෙය්‌ ප්‍රතිපාදන වලට අදාළ ඉතුරැ මුදල විලමිභීත ආදායම්‌
ලෙස පිළිගනු ලබන අතර වෙනත්‌ විලම්භීත නොවන වගකිම්‌ යටතේ

රැ. 23, 559,826.80 ක මුදල ඉදිරිපත්‌ කෙරේ.

සටහන 26 - අදාල පාර්ශවයේ අනාවරණය කිරීම්‌

A.   ධීවර හා ජලජ සම්පත්‌ සංවර්ධන අමාත්‍යාංශයට අනුබද්ධව කියාත්මක වන
සීමාසහිත සීනොෝට පදනමහට එම අමාත්‍යාංශය මගින්‌ සහ එයට අනුබද්ධිත
අනෙකුත්‌ ආයතන වලින්‌ ලබා දී ඇති ඇණවුම්‌ මගින්‌ රැ. 123,409, 863.72 ක

මුදලක්‌ 2017 වර්ෂය තුල උපයා ඇත.

B.    සීමාසහිත සීනොෝරී පදනමෙහි සභාපති ලෙස සේවය කරන පදනමෙහි ගණන්දීමේ
නිලධාරියා එම අමාත්‍යාංශයට අනුබද්ධිත ධිවර සංස්ථාවෙහි සභාපති හා ජාතික
ජලජීවී අධිකාරියේ අධ්‍යක්ෂ මණ්ඩල සාමාජිකයෙකු ලෙස කියා කරයි.

C.   සීමාසහිත සීනෝරී පදනම 2008 වර්ෂයේ බන්ග්ලාදේශයේ පිහිටි ශී බංග්ලාස්‌
බෝටිටූ පුද්ගලික ආයතනය සමග රැ. 1 961 850.00 ක ආයෝජනයක්‌ සහිතව

ආරම්භ කරන ලද බෝට්ටු සෑදීම ව්‍යාපාරයෙහි අධ්‍යක්ෂ මණ්ඩලය සීනොෝරී
පදනමෙහි අධ්‍යක්ෂකවරයන්‌ දෙදෙනෙකුගෙන්ද සමන්විත විය යුතු බව සඳහන්‌ කර
ඇත.

සටහන 27 - වෙන්‌ කිරීම්‌ සහ විලම්භිත බැරකම්‌

වර්ෂ 2017 තුල දී සමාගම විසින්‌ නිෂ්පාදනය කරන ලද ෆයිබර්‌ බෝට්ටු සඳහා වගකීම්‌
සහතික නිකුත්‌ කිරීම සමාගමට විලමිභීත බැරකමකි. ආර්ථික වාසිය නැති වීම නිසා හෝ
ජලය කාන්දු වීමේ ප්‍රවණතාවය නිසා හෝ මේ දක්වා වගකිම්‌ සඳහා    කිසිම
ගනුදෙනුකරැවක ඉල්ලම්‌ කර නැත.

සටහන 28 - ආයෝජන දේපලෙන්‌ ලැබෙන ආදායම

සමාගම ආයෝජන ගණනය කිරීම සඳහා ආදරශ පිරවැයක්‌ යොදාගන්නා ලදී.
විශ්වාසනීයත්වය තීරණය කිරීමට සාධාරණ වටිනා කමකින්‌ යුතු බද ආදායමක්‌ 2017
වර්ෂයට ලබා ගැනීමට ආයෝජන දේපලෙන්‌ පහත දක්වා ඇති ක්‍රමයට ඇස්තමේන්තු කළ
පිරිවැයක්‌ යොදා ගන්නා ලදී.

VISSION, MISSION, OBJECTIVES

VISION

To be the market leader in building of fishing and leisure crafts and supplying fishnet
and fishing gears.

MISSION

Operating as an efficient and effective government owned company which supplies
high standard fishing crafts and fishing gears at competitive prices.

OBJECTIVES

> To become a recognized exporter of fiberglass boats.
> To become afiberglass boat builder of international repute
> Tobe an excellent customer services provider.

> To be an effective contributor to the development of Fishing mdustry by

supplying high quality fiberglass products.

04


INTRODUCTION

Cey Nor Foundation Limited was incorporated as a Public Limited Liability Company

on 17 January 1000 to take over and carry on the business of the Government
Owned Business undertaking of Cey Nor Development Foundation Limited, under
the Conversion of Public Corporations or Government Owned Business
Undertakings into Public Companies Act No. 23 of 1087.

The Cey Nor Development Foundation began operations in 10967, as a nonprofit
organization dedicated to enhancing the education and welfare of the domestic
fishing community.

Over the years the organization has undergone several transformation as
Summarized below.

1067     —      Cey Nor Development Foundation was created and
began operations, utilizing the aid received from
NORGES GODTEMPLAR UNGDOMS FORBUND (NGU)-a
Norwegian Non-Governmental Organization.

1071        —           Incorporated under the Companies Ordinance No. 51 of
1038 as a Public Company Limited by guarantee and
was known as Cey-Nor Development Foundation
Limited.

1085         —             Acquired by the Government of Sri Lanka under the
Business Acquisition Act No: 35 of 1071 and became the
GOBU of Cey-Nor Development Foundation Limited.

1000       —            The GOBU of Cey-Nor Development Foundation ceased
to exist with the application of the Conversion of Public
Corporations or GOBU into Public Companies Act No. 23
of 1087.

Cey Nor Foundation Limited was incorporated under
the Companies Act No. 17 of 190872, to succeed the former
GOBU of Cey Nor Development Foundation Limited.

2011    —        Two Net Factories belonged to Cey Nor Foundation
Limited at Lunuwila & Weerawila was transferred to
North Sea Limited & North Sea Limited Handed Over
demolished Karainagar boat yard to Cey Nor
Foundation Limited.

05


Annual Report                                                                                                              2017

2013    —        Mattakkuliya boat yard was upgraded with modern
tools and equipment to provide services to all kinds of
vessels.

Entire share capital of this new company (Rs. 40,000,000) has been allotted to the
Secretary to the Treasury.

Initially the activities of the Company were limited to the manufacture and repair of
boats at Karainagar Boat Yard. Over the years the Company expanded its activities;
however, in the 1900s the Company was forced to cease certain activities due to
operational difficulties and the unsettled situation prevailed in the country.
Gurunagar Fish Net Factory which was closed in 1001 remained under Cey Nor till
30.00.2001. Now this Factory functions under the name of “North Sea Limited”,
comes under the Ministry of Rehabilitation of the North.

006


CHAIRMAN’S REVIEW

It is great pleasure me to submit successfully concluded Annual Report for the
financial year ended at 31st December 2017 to cabinet of ministries, after achieving
very good results of the projects, we laid up in 2016 for continuous and stable
progress of Cey Nor Foundation.

In the first quarter of 2017, we successfully completed constructions of 59.5 feet
mould of the multiday boat, started in 2016 as per a concept of Hon. Minister
Mahinda Amaraweera to minimize post-harvest loss experiencing by the fisheries
communities in Sri Lanka.

Cey Nor started construction of five trawlers with modern freezing, fish finding and
gathering equipment in 2017 with the support and directives given by the Hon.
Minister, Secretary and Director General of Department of Fisheries & Aquatic
Resources Development.

In addition Cey Nor was given an opportunity to monitor the construction of another
five multiday boats as a consultant, constructed by the private sector boat yards on
the request of beneficiaries selected by the Departments of Fisheries.

In 2016 we started renovation of ruined warehouse complex in Mattakkuliya Boat
Yard, spending more than 1.2 M and successfully completed construction in first
quarter of 2017. By following government procurement procedures we rented out
renovated warehouse complex (25,000 square feet) to Anverraly & Sons Company
Itd, above the government valuation.

Except to construction of multiday trawlers, in 2017 we successfully completed
construction of 150 numbers of 19.5 feet long flat bottom boats offered by Indian
High Commission for the fishermen in Mulathive in Northern Zone.

In view of motivating and gaining maximum output from our staff, in 2017 we
introduced following benefits to increase the welfare of Cey Nor Staff.

01. Group health insurance policy including family members.
02. Dust allowance for Boatyard workers.

03. Transport allowances for Managers.

04. Telephone allowances for Managers.

05. Professional allowances for managers.

In 2018, we have strengthen our system and procedures to avoid weakness
mentioned in Auditor General's report for the financial year ended 31st December
2017.


Tam thankful to the Hon. Mahinda Amaraweera, the Minister of Fisheries and Aquatic
Resources Development for the guidance and assistance to achieve the objects of the
Company in the year 2016. I am grateful to the cooperation extended by the staft of
the line Ministry of Fisheries and Aquatic Resources Development in dealing with
various matters of Company throughout the year. Further, I am also thankful to the
Board of Director and members of staff at all levels of the Company who assisted me
in making the Company Success towards its goals during the year.

\
B.K.Jagath Perera
Chairman
Ceynor Foundation Limited

ACHIEVEMENTS OF THE YEAR 2017

In relation to the business and
operational activities compared to
2014 and 2015, in the year
2017also steps had been taken to
carry out all business activities
based on the objectives of the
establishment of the company.
During the year 2014 and2015,
company was able to earn an
additional income by entering into
the maritime construction besides
the income generated through
production and sale of fishing
vessels and fishing gear.

The main objective of establishing
the company of operational affairs
in year 2017 is the production of
fishing boats, leisure boats and
fishing gear. Actions have been
taken to manufacture fishing boats
and other fishing gear with high
quality and which are contributed
to enhance the field of fishery by
only limiting those productions. In
year 2017, The Company has
fulfilled to achieve the expected
target.

lol 4 ge |e)

Il


Annual Report                                                            2017

Ministry of Fisheries and Aquatic Resources Development has planned to develop
Freshwater Fishery as well as maritime Fishery and generate a great number of
employments opportunities. Hence, action has been taken to provide a huge amount of
canoes, out-trigger and fish packing boxes to fishermen who engage in fishing in the river
related Freshwater Fishery and Steps have been taken by the National Aquaculture
Development Authority of Sri Lanka to hand over all these orders to the Cey Nor
Foundation Limited. In 2016, Cey Nor Foundation Limited achieved very good revenue
by producing lots of canoes, out-trigger and fish keeping boxes by these orders.

The investigations of NARA have been revealed that the fish harvest has not been
properly packed with ice therefore a large number of fish harvest lost. Therefore, in2010,
we have entered to manufacture fish keeping boxes which can be stored safely the fish
harvest to minimize the post - harvest lost.

I2


Annual Report                                                            2017

In accordance to the instructions of Hon. Mahinda Amaraweera, the Minister of Fisheries
and Aquatic Resources Development, investigation activities had been commenced in
2016 to find remedies for wasting post- harvest experience for long time by the fishers
engage in the maritime industry.

We have noticed that the length of fishing boats, the quantity of fish holds, freezer facility
and weakness of packing the harvested fish were the major factors for wasting post -
harvest.

In accordance to the proposal submitted by the Cey Nor Foundation Limited to the
Cabinet of Ministers in 2016 last quarter, action has been taken to grant Rs.44 Million to
the Cey Nor Foundation Limited through Department of Fisheries and Aquatic Resources
Development to make mould of 55 Feet vessel and manufacture prototype vessel by using
this mould for minimizing post - harvest. Action has also been taken to demonstrate it for
fishers of Sri Lanka. In 2017, Cey Nor successfully completed the construction of 59.5 feet
long mould and 55 feet long prototype multiday boat.

13


Annual Report                                                          2017

Under the vote of introducing new technology in line with the project, Department of
Fisheries and Aquatic Resources Development has taken action to provide orders to
Cey Nor Foundation Limited to manufacture five vessels using the mould manufactured
by us under 50% assistance introducing by the Department of Fisheries and Aquatic
Resources Development for the manufacture of vessels more than 55 Feet vessels.

In addition to manufacture vessels and other fishing gear which are necessary to fishery,
we have successfully completed the manufacture activities of Shashimi type two whale
watching boats which are facilitated to travel more than 100 passengers and length of
50ft manufactured by only on Cey Nor Foundation Limited and handed over to the
owners. These boats have high demand in the tourism industry.

TURE PLANS TT

Cey Nor Foundation renovated the ruined warehouse complex situated in mattakkuliya
by spending 12M in 2016. The board of directors expects to rent out the renovated
warehouse Complex to a perspective bidder subject to approved procurement
procedures and government valuation.

The board of directors expect to start
operation of newly build Karainagar
Boatyard with collaboration of prospective
private investor.

The board of directors are considering to increase the monthly rent value of the
Maththumagala workshop, with Frontier Automotive Mobile, above the proceed
government valuation.

The management agreement with orient pearl hotel for the land at No. 335 /A,
D. R. Wijewardhana Mawatha, Colombo 10 is due to expire in this year. The board of
directors expects to enhance the period subject to cabinet approval and government
valuations.

We have planned to get the maximum use of the air conditioned room, paramaraine
software and other high tech equipment donated by Dikkowita harbor project. The board
of directors arranged to recruit qualified personals, in order to operate the high tech
equipment.

Cey-Nor Foundation Limited

Report of the Auditor General on the Financial Statements of the Cey-Nor Foundation
Limited for the year ended 31 December 2017

The audit of financial statements of the Cey-Nor Foundation Limited for the year ended 31
December 2017 comprising the statement of financial position as at 31 December 2017 and
the comprehensive income statement, statement of changes in equity and cash flow statement
for the year then ended and a summary of significant accounting policies and other
explanatory information, was Carried out under my direction in pursuance of provisions in

Article 154(1) of the Constitution of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka.

Responsibility of the Board of Directors for the Financial Statements

The Board of Directors is responsible for the preparation and fair presentation of these
financial statements in accordance with Sri Lanka Accounting Standards and for such internal
control as the Board of Directors determines is necessary to enable the preparation of

financial statements that are free from material misstatements. whether due to fraud or error.

Auditor’s Responsibility

My responsibility is to express an opinion on these financial statements based on my audit. I
conducted my audit in accordance with Sri Lanka Auditing Standards. Those Standards
require that I comply with ethical requirements and plan and perform the audit to obtain
reasonable assurance about whether the financial statements are free from material

misstatements.

An audit involves performing procedures to obtain audit evidence about the amounts and
disclosures in the financial statements. The procedures selected depend on the auditor's
judgement, including the assessment of the risks of material misstatement of the financial
Statements, whether duc to fraud or crror. In making those risk assessments, the auditor
considers internal control relevant to the Foundation’s preparation and fair presentation of the
financial statements in order to design audit procedures that are appropriate in the
circumstances. but not for the purpose of expressing an opinion on the effectiveness of the
Foundation’s internal control. An audit also includes cvaluating the appropriateness of

accounting policies used and the reasonableness of accounting estimates made by

management, as well as evaluating the overall presentation of financial statements.

I believe that the audit evidence TI have obtained is sufficient and appropriate to provide a

basis for my audit opinion.
Basis for Qualified Opinion

(a)     The Sri Bangalas Boats Manufacturing Company, which was commenced according
to an agreement entered into with an investor of Bangladesh by the Cey-Nor
Foundation Limited on 14 February 2008. was running at a loss and as such. the
agreement had been terminated on the decision dated 23 July 2016 of the Board of
Directors. However, according to Sri Lanka Accounting Standard 36. allocations had
not been made for impairment of investment of Rs.l.061.850 remained as at 31

December 2017.

(b)      Even though the Ambulance Boat valucd at Rs.4.822,544 manufactured by the
Foundation in the year 2015 at the request of the buyer. had not been transferred even
by the year 2016 to the relevant buyer, it had been adjusted to the sales income of the
year under review instead of adjusting to the profit of the preceding year regarding the
rectification of accounting it as sales income on 07 December 2015, thus understating
the profit of the year under review by Rs.4.822.544. Further, the accuracy of the
closing stock balance of the year under review could not be satisfied in audit due to
failure in taking action to climinate the cost of the boat from the stock. Even though
It had been decided at the meeting of the Board of Directors held on 23 June 2017 to
Sell the said boat as scrap, the Foundation had not taken action even to make adequate

provisions for losses in stocks that may occur.

(0)     The Foundation had entered into an agreement on 00 November 2017 with a private
institution to manufacture and supply a ferry valued at Rs.8.741.820 and to pay an
advance of 20 per cent therefor. Even though the said ferry which was incomplete
even by 31 March 2010 by spending Rs.2.5 million had not been transferred to the
buyer, it had been brought to account on 31 October 2017 considering as sales income
of Rs.8.741.820. As such, the revenue of the year under review and the debtors
balance as at 31 December 2017 had been overstated by Rs.§.741.820 in the financial

Statements.

(dD      The value of mobile workshops by which an income of Rs. 1.241.176 had been earned
for the year 2017, had not been included in the financial statements of the Foundation

by recognizing as properties.

(©)    It was observed in audit that only provisions of Rs.6.,302.400 had been made for
debtors totalling Rs.57.261.804 as at 31 December 2017 remained unrecovered in the
years 2004. 2011 and 2015 without making adequate provisions for doubtful debts for

them.

(D      The deeds or valuation reports required for the confirmation of the ownership and the
cost of the Mattumagala land in a reliable manner, valued at Rs.115.000.000 shown
under properties. plant and equipment in the financial statements, had not been made

available to Audit.

(@)     According to the Nation Building Tax Returns and financial statements, the Nation
Building Tax payable as at 31 December 2017 had been overstated by Rs.9,630,013
and information to explain the related year for which the negative payable balance of
value added tax amounting to Rs.7.420.,048 remaining in the financial statements

since the preceding. years, had not been available with the Foundation.

(hh    The balance of Rs.2.078.302 out of Government grants amounting to Rs.20 million
provided by the Ministry of Fisheries and Aquatic Resources Development in the year
2010 for creating a boat mould for the Boat Yard at Mattakkuliya had been shown as
a balance to be settled to the Ministry in the financial statements for the year ended 31
December 2017. However, relevant source documents were not available with the

Foundation.

(D      The debtors balance oft Rs.11.333.770 had been shown as at 31 December 2017 in the
financial statements of the Foundation in the name of Ministry of Fisheries. National
Aquatic Resources Research and Development Agency and National Aquaculture
Development Authority. However, the financial statements of those institutions
proved that there were no such balances. As such, the accuracy of the debtors
balance amounting to Rs.11.333.779 shown in the financial statements, cannot be

Satisfied in Audit

i)   The information on creditors totalling Rs.1.385.420 included in Trade Debtors
remained as at 31 December 2017 and confirmation of balances relating to selected
35 creditors totalling Rs.32.684.000 had not been received to Audit. As such. the

accuracy of the creditors balance totalling Rs.34.070.32° cannot be satisfied in Audit.

(R)    The creditors balance of Rs.533.130 remained as at 31 December 2017 had been
confirmed as a zero balance by the relevant institution. As such. the accuracy of the
Said balance cannot be satisfied in Audit.

(D    The Foundation had failed to submit investigation reports and lease agreements in
respect of a sum of Rs.1.802.572 remained for a long period under other receivables

in the financial statements of the year under review.

(m) The fishing nets valued only at Rs.140,275 which were manufactured by using raw
materials valued at Rs.5.059,050 provided for manufacturing of fishing nets on sub-
contract basis awarded to a private institution in the year 2011. had been received by
the Foundation. As such, the remaining raw materials valued at Rs.4.000.775 or 97
per cent had been shown under receivables of the financial statements without taking
action to settle them since the year 2011. However. the Foundation had failed to

Submit the contract agreement entered into in this connection.

(mn)    A diftcrence of Rs.4.848.,844 was observed between the balance of provisions for
accumulated depreciation .remained as at 31 December 2017 according to the
schedules of computation of depreciation presented to Audit by the Foundation and
the balance of provisions for accumulated depreciation indicated in the financial

Statements.

(0)      Even though sums of Rs.26.204.662 and Rs. 1§.010.,833 had been shown under current
assets and trade creditors in the name of Northsea Limited in the financial statements
of the Cey-Nor Foundation Limited as at 31 December 2017, according to the
financial statements of the Northsea Limited. a sum of Rs.2.101.13§8 had been
indicated only under trade creditors. As such. the accuracy of balances of
Rs.2 6.204.062 and Rs.15.009.605 shown under current assets and trade debtors in the

financial statements of the Foundation. cannot be satisfied in Audit.

Qualified Opinion

In my opinion, except for the efrects of the matters described in paragraph on the basis for
qualified opinion of this report.  the financial statements give a true and fair view of the
financial position of the Cey-Nor Foundation Limited as at 31 December 2017 and its
financial performance and cash flows for the year then ended in accordance with Sri Lanka

Accounting Standards.

Report on other Legal and Regulatory Requirements

As required by Section 163(2) of the Companies Act, No. 7 of 2007, I'state the followings:

(a)    The basis of qualified opinion and scope and limitations of the audit are as
Stated above.
(bh)       In my opinion;            |
Ihave obtained all the information and explanations that were required
for the audit and as far as appears from my examination, proper
accounting records have been kept by the Foundation and:
the financial statements of the Company comply with the requirements

of Section 151 of the Companies Act. No. 7 of 2007.

Tabling of Annual Reports
In terms of provisions of the Article 154(0) of the Constitution of the Democratic Socialist

Republic of Sri Lanka. my report will be tabled in Parliament in due course.

CEY NOR FOUNDATION LIMITED NOTES TO THE FINANCIAL STATEMENTS

YEAR ENDED 315°T DECEMBER 2017

1

Corporate Information

1.1 Domicile and Legal Form

Cey-Nor Foundation Limited is a limited liability Company incorporated and
domiciled in Sri Lanka. The Registered Office of the Company is located at No. 335,
D.R.Wijewardana Mawatha, Colombo-10 and the factory is located at Mattakkuliya.

1.2 Principal Activities and Nature of Operations

During the year, the principal activities of the Company were and sale of
manufactured fishing boats, other fiber glass products and sale of imported and
locally purchased fishing nets.

1.3       Parent Enterprise
A 100% Government owned Company.

Number of Employees
The number of employees of the Company at the end of the year was 87

Summary of Significant Accounting Policies

2.1 General Policies

2.1.1 Basis of Preparation

The Statement of Financial Position, Statement of Comprehensive Income, Changes
in equity and cash flows, together with accounting policies and notes (‘financial
statements”) of the Company as at 31st December 2017 and for the year then
ended, comply with the Sri Lanka Accounting Standards.

These financial statements presented in Sri Lanka rupees have been
prepared on a historical cost basis, except where otherwise stated in the
accounting policies below. No adjustment is made for inflationary factors
affecting these financial statements.

2.1.2 Changes in Accounting Policies and Adoption of new and Revised Sri Lanka
Accounting Standards during the year.

The accounting policies adopted are consistent with those of the previous financial
year.

2.1.3 Comparative Imformation

The accounting policies have been consistently applied by the Company and are
consistent with those used in the previous year. Previous year figures and phrases
have been rearranged wherever necessary to confirm to the current presentation.

30


2.1.4

2.1.5

2.1.0

2.1.7

2.2

2.2.1

Foreign Currency Transactions

All foreign exchange transactions are converted to Sri Lanka rupee, which is the
reporting currency, at the rate of exchange prevailing at the time the transactions
were effected. Monetary assets and liabilities denominated in foreign currencies
are re-measured to Sri Lanka Rupee equivalents using year-end spot foreign
exchange rates. The resulting gains and losses, if any, are accounted for in the
Statement of comprehensive.

Taxation
Current Taxes

The provision for income tax is based on the elements of income and expenditure
as reported in the financial statements and computed in accordance with the
provisions of the Inland Revenue Act No. 10 of 2006 at the current rate applicable
to this company

Events after the Reporting Period

All material events after the reporting date have been considered and where
necessary adjustments have been made in the financial statements.

Borrowing Costs

Borrowing costs are recognized as an expense in the period in which they are
incurred.

Valuation of Assets and Their Measurement Bases

Imventories

Inventories are valued at the lower of cost and net realizable value, after making
que allowances for obsolete and slow moving items. Net realizable value is the
price at which inventories can be sold in the ordinary course of business less the
estimated cost of completion and the estimated cost necessary to make the sale.
The cost incurred in bringing inventories to its present location and condition is
accounted using the following cost formulae:

Raw Materials                               - At actual cost on first — in first — out basis

Manufactured Finished Goods     - At actual cost of direct materials, direct labour and an

appropriate proportion of fixed production overheads

Work-in-Progress                 - At actual cost of direct materials, direct labour and an

appropriate proportion of fixed production overheads
based on percentage completed.

Finished Goods Purchased             - At actual cost on first — in first — out basis

Other Stocks                                  - At actual cost on first — in first — out basis

40


2.2L.

Financial assets

Trade and other receivables are initially recognized at the transaction price.
All sales are made on the basis of normal credit terms, and the receivables
do not bear interest. At the end of each reporting period, the carrying
amounts of trade and other receivables are reviewed to determine whether
there is any objective evidence that the amounts are not recoverable. If so,
an impairment loss is recognized immediately in profit or loss.

Cash and cash equivalents are defined as cash in hand, demand deposits and short
term highly liquid investments, readily convertible to known amounts of cash and
without subject to insignificant risk of changes in value.

For the purpose of cash flow statement, cash and cash equivalents consist of cash
in hand and deposits in banks net of outstanding bank overdrafts, investments
with short maturities, i.e. three months or less from the date of acquisition are also
treated as cash equivalents.

2.2.3. Property, Plant and Equipment

a)

b)

Cost of Valuation

All items of property, plant and equipment are initially measured at cost. The
cost of property, plant and equipment is the cost of purchase or construction
together with all such expenditure incidental to bringing the asset to its present
condition and location.

Property, plant and equipment are subsequently measured at cost less
accumulated depreciation and accumulated impairment loses.

Subsequent expenditure on acquisition and improvement of property, plant
and equipment are capitalized only when it increases the standard of
performance of these assets and the future economic benefits embodied in
these assets will flow to the company.

Depreciation

The provision for depreciation is calculated on cost on a straight line basis for
all property, plant and equipment in order to write off such amounts over the
estimated useful lives. The useful lives of each asset classes are stated below:

Buildings                               20 Years
Plant and machinery               10 Years
Furniture and fittings             05 Years
Tools and equipments            05 Years
Office equipments                  05 Years
Motor vehicles                          04 Years
Computers                                 04 Years
Software                               05 Years
Boat moulds                            05 Years
Factory equipments                 08 Years
Leasehold Motor vehicles         04 Years

41


Impairment of Non-Financial Assets

At each reporting date, properties are reviewed to determine whether
there is any indication that those assets have suffered an impairment
loss. If there is an indication of possible impairment, the recoverable
amount of any affected asset (or group of related assets) is estimated and
compared with its carrying amount. If the estimated recoverable amount
is lower, the carrying amount is reduced to its estimated recoverable
amount, and an impairment loss is recognized immediately in the
Statement of Other Comprehensive Income.

If an impairment loss for a non-financial asset other than goodwill
subsequently reverses, the carrying amount of the asset (or group of
related assets) is increased to the revised estimate of its recoverable
amount, but not in excess of the amount that would have been
determined had no impairment loss been recognized for the asset (or
group of related assets) in prior years. A reversal of an impairment loss
is recognized immediately in the Statement of Other Comprehensive
Income.

2.3 Liabilities and Provisions

2.3.1.

a)

b)

Retirement Benefit Obligations
Defined Benefit Plan — Gratuity

Gratuity is a Defined Benefit plan. The Company is liable to pay gratuity in terms
of the relevant statute. In order to meet this liability, a provision is carried forward
in the Statement of Financial Position, equivalent to an amount calculated based
on a half month's salary of the last month of the financial year ofall employees for
each completed year of service, from the date of commencement of service. The
resulting difference between brought forward provision at the beginning of the
year and the carried forward provision at the end of the year is dealt with in the
Statement of Other Comprehensive Income.

However, as per the payment of Gratuity Act No. 12 of 1083, this liability only
arises upon completion of five (05) years of continued service. The gratuity
liability is not funded nor actuarially valued. This item is grouped under Deferred
Liabilities in the Statement of Financial Position.

Defined Contribution Plans — Employees’ Provident Fund and Employees’
Trust Fund

All employees who are eligible for Employees’ Provident Fund Contribution and
Employees’ Trust Fund Contribution are covered by relevant contribution funds in
line with respective statutes and regulations.

Employees’ Provident Fund

The company and employees contribute 12% and 8% respectively on the
salary of each employee to the approved Provident Fund.

42


2.3.2

2.3.3

2.3.4

Employees’ Trust Fund

The company contributes 3% of the salary of each employee to the
Employees’ Trust Fund.

Financial Liabilities

Financial liabilities are initially recognized at the transaction price
(including transaction costs). Payables are obligations on the basis of
normal credit terms and do not bear interest.

Capital Commitments and Contingencies

Capital commitments and contingent liabilities as at the reporting date are
disclosed in the notes to the financial statements (ref note no. 27).

Provisions

Provisions are recognized when the Company has a present obligation (legal
or constructive) as a result of a past event, it is probable that the Company
will be required to settle the obligation, and a reliable estimate can be made
of the amount of the obligation.

The amount recognized as a provision is the best estimate of the
consideration required to settle the present obligation at the statement of
financial position date, taking into account the risks and uncertainties
surrounding the obligation. Where a provision is measured using the cash
flows estimated to settle the present obligation, its carrying amount is the
present value of those cash flows.

2.4. Imcome Statements

2.4.1

Revenue Recognition

Revenue is recognized to the extent that it is probable that the economic benefits
will flow to the Company and the revenue and associated costs incurred or to be
incurred can be reliably measured. Revenue is measured at the fair value of the
consideration received or receivable net of trade discounts and sales taxes. The
company does not retains significant risk of ownership even though warranties
are provided for its’ manufactured items, since that warranties covers only the
manufacturing defects which covered under normal warranty provisions. The
following specific criteria are used for the purpose of recognition of revenue.

a)         Sale of Goods

Revenue from sale of goods is recognized when the significant risk and
rewards of ownership of the goods have passed to buyer with the Company
retaining neither continuing managerial involvement to the degree usually
associated with ownership, nor effective control over the goods sold.

b)          Imterest

Interest income is recognized on an accrual basis.

Rental Income
Rental income is recognized on an accrual basis.

a)         Other Income

Other income is recognized on an accrual basis.

43


e)         Gains and Losses

2.4.2

a)

b)

Net gains and losses ofa revenue nature on the disposal of property, plantand
equipment are accounted for in the statement of other comprehensive
income, after deducting from proceeds on disposal, the carrying amount of
the assets and related selling expenses on disposal of relevant property, plant
and equipment. The amount remaining in the revaluation reserve relating to
that asset is transferred directly to accumulated profits.

Government Grants

The grantis recognized when there is reasonable assurance that company will
comply with the conditions attached and that government grant will be
received.

Grants related to assets, recognized as deferred income that is recognized in
profit or loss over the periods and in the proportions in which depreciation
expense on those assets is recognized.

Expenditure Recognition

Expenses are recognized in the income statement on the basis of a direct association
between the cost incurred and the earning of specific items of income. Al
expenditure incurred in the running of the business and in maintaining the
property, plat and equipment in a state of efficiency has been charged to income
Statement in arriving at the profit for the year.

For the purpose of presentation of the statement of other comprehensive income,
the company has adopted the function of expenses method, on the basis that it
presents fairly the elements of the company’s performance.

2.4.3 Critical Judgment and Key Sources of Estimation Uncertainty

The preparation of the company’s financial statements require
management to make judgments, estimates and assumptions that effect the
reported amounts of revenue, expenses, assets and liabilities and the
disclose of contingent liabilities at the reporting date. Actual results may
differ from these estimates.

Note 25 —
Government Grant

A. Government grant relating to assets has recognized in the Statement of Comprehensive
Income over the useful life of the particular assets. During this financial year,
Rs. 11,315,087.890 has been recognized in the Statement of Comprehensive Income
under “Other Operating Income”. The balance amount of government grant, which is not
recognized as an income during the period, is recognized as deferred income and
presented under “Other Non-Deferred Liabilities” and the amount is Rs. 23,559,826.80.

Note 26 -

Related Party Disclosure

Cey- Nor Foundation has earned Rs.123,4909,863.72 in year 2017 from Ministry of
Fisheries and Aquatic Resources Development and the other institutions pertaining to
the ministry, which considered as government related entities as the company is
functioning under the same ministry.

A.

B. Chairman of the Cey Nor Foundation Ltd, who is considered as a Key Management
Personnel is the same personnel who worked as the chairman of the Ceylon Fisheries
Corporation and represent as a member of the Board of Directors of the National
Aquaculture Development Authority which are functioning under the same ministry.

C.   Company has entered to a joint venture agreement on 14th day of February 2008 named as
Sribanglas Boats (Pvt) Limited, a company located at Bangladesh, with the investment of Rs
1,961,850 with main purpose of building fiber glass boats which was considered as a related
party which the Board of directors has to be constituted with two members, one from each party.

Note 27 —
Provision and Contingent
Liabilities

In year 2017, the company has given warranty certificates for a one year period for fiber
glass products which is a contingent liability to the company. Nevertheless customers
has never claimed the warranty, the possibility of an outflow of resources embodying
economic benefit is remote.

Properties
